<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pear_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:pear (disambiguation)">pear</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pear_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:pear (disambiguation)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Pears.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pears.jpg/220px-Pears.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="335" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pears.jpg/330px-Pears.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Pears.jpg/440px-Pears.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="975"></a><figcaption>Photo of a pair of <b>pears</b> on a tree</figcaption></figure>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/pere#Middle_English" title="pere">pere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/pere#Old_English" title="pere">pere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-West_Germanic/peru" title="Reconstruction:Proto-West Germanic/peru">*peru</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Latin/pira&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Latin/pira (page does not exist)">*pira</a></i>, originally the plural of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/pirum#Latin" title="pirum">pirum</a></i> but reconstrued as a feminine singular, ultimately a loanword from an unknown Mediterranean <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Stratum_(linguistics)" class="extiw" title="w:Stratum (linguistics)">substrate</a></span> source. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Saterland_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Saterland Frisian language">Saterland Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="stq"><a href="/wiki/Peere#Saterland_Frisian" title="Peere">Peere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href="/wiki/peer#Dutch" title="peer">peer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A6re#Danish" title="pære">pære</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href="/wiki/poire#French" title="poire">poire</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Birne#German" title="Birne">Birne</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is"><a href="/wiki/pera#Icelandic" title="pera">pera</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A4ron#Swedish" title="päron">päron</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pear" class="extiw" title="w:pear">pear</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pear" class="extiw" title="w:pear">Wikipedia </a></span></div>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pear</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pears#English" title="pears">pears</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>An edible fruit produced by the pear tree, similar to an <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/apple#English" title="apple">apple</a> but typically elongated towards the stem.</li>
<li>A type of fruit tree (<span class="biota"><a href="/wiki/Pyrus_communis#Translingual" title="Pyrus communis"><i>Pyrus communis</i></a></span>).
<span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pear_tree#English" title="pear tree">pear tree</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The wood of the pear tree (<a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pearwood#English" title="pearwood">pearwood</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=pear_wood&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pear wood (page does not exist)">pear wood</a>).</li>
<li><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/choke_pear#English" title="choke pear">Choke pear</a> (a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/torture#English" title="torture">torture</a> device).</li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jamaican_English" class="extiw" title="w:Jamaican English">Jamaica</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/avocado#English" title="avocado">avocado</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/alligator_pear#English" title="alligator pear">alligator pear</a></li>
<li>A desaturated <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/chartreuse#English" title="chartreuse">chartreuse</a> yellow <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/colour#English" title="colour">colour</a>, like that of a pear.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">pear: <span style="background-color:#D1E231; display:inline-block; width:80px;">&nbsp;</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*pilare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/pila#Latin" title="pila">pīla</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pillar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_2">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pear&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="gl">pear</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-gl p-form-of" lang="gl"><a href="/wiki/peares#Galician" title="peares">peares</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pillar#English" title="pillar">pillar</a>
<span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="gl"><a href="/wiki/columna#Galician" title="columna">columna</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/window#English" title="window">window</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/sill#English" title="sill">sill</a>
<span class="nyms-toggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="gl"><a href="/wiki/peitoril#Galician" title="peitoril">peitoril</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>one of several <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/stone#English" title="stone">stone</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/pillar#English" title="pillar">pillars</a> placed by way of a <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/bridge#English" title="bridge">bridge</a>
